    class OpenSearchQueryParamBuilder {
        +get_sort_column()
        +get_order_direction()

        +get_current_location_code_filter_clause()
        +get_final_mile_origin_location_code_filter_clause()
        +get_delivery_date_clause()
    }
    class TestLastMilestoneFilter {
        +test_last_milestone_exact_match()
        +test_last_milestone_is_null()
        +test_last_milestone_is_not_null()
    }
    class TestCurrentLocationFilter {
        +test_current_location_exact_match()
        +test_current_location_is_null()
        +test_current_location_is_not_null()
    }
    class TestFinalMileOriginFilter {
        +test_final_mile_origin_exact_match()
        +test_final_mile_origin_is_null()
        +test_final_mile_origin_is_not_null()
    }
    class TestDeliveryDateFilter {
        +test_delivery_date_with_valid_date_range()
        +test_delivery_date_with_none_delivery_date_type()
        +test_delivery_date_with_empty_string_delivery_date_type()
        +test_delivery_date_with_invalid_delivery_date_type()
        +test_delivery_date_with_valid_single_type()
    }
    TestLastMilestoneFilter ..> OpenSearchQueryParamBuilder
    TestCurrentLocationFilter ..> OpenSearchQueryParamBuilder
    TestFinalMileOriginFilter ..> OpenSearchQueryParamBuilder
    TestDeliveryDateFilter ..> OpenSearchQueryParamBuilder

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> ParamsProvided
    ParamsProvided --> ValidateSortColumn
    ValidateSortColumn --> ValidColumn: sortColumn in SortKey
    ValidateSortColumn --> DefaultColumn: invalid/None sortColumn
    ValidColumn --> DetermineOrder
    DefaultColumn --> DetermineOrder
    DetermineOrder --> AscOrder: reverseSort=False
    DetermineOrder --> DescOrder: reverseSort=True
    AscOrder --> BuildOrderByClause
    DescOrder --> BuildOrderByClause
    BuildOrderByClause --> [*]
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    A[Filter Params] --> B{Check Filter Type}
    B -->|Code Value| C[Exact Match Query]
    B -->|Empty Flag| D[Must Not Exists]
    B -->|IsNotEmpty Flag| E[Must Exists]
    C --> F[Return query, must]
    D --> G[Return query, must_not]
    E --> F
```

## Diagram 6

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> CheckDeliveryDateType
    CheckDeliveryDateType --> None_Type: deliveryDateType is None
    CheckDeliveryDateType --> Empty_Type: deliveryDateType is ""
    CheckDeliveryDateType --> Invalid_Type: invalid type
    CheckDeliveryDateType --> Valid_Type: valid type
    None_Type --> ReturnNone
    Empty_Type --> ReturnNone
    Invalid_Type --> ReturnNone
    Valid_Type --> BuildRangeQuery
    BuildRangeQuery --> ReturnClause
    ReturnNone --> [*]
    ReturnClause --> [*]
```
